Xim Sansにおいて私用領域などに存在しているUnicode未登録文字をUnicode公式っぽく紹介します。
いくつか「にしき的フォント」や「Quivira」などの他フォントに含まれている文字もあるため、参考としてそちらも参照しております。

なお、これらの文字を入力する時は日本語入力モードなら「Unicode値＋F5キー」でUnicode値から文字を入力できるので便利。

#	Latin Extended Private-1
##	Latin extensions for Koalib
	U+E000
　LATIN  CAPITAL LETTER AT
　　https://unicode.org/L2/L2019/19006-capital-at.pdf
　　•used for Koalib
　　•F248 in nishiki-teki font
　　•F004 in Quivira
	U+E001
　LATIN  SMALL LETTER AT
　　https://unicode.org/L2/L2019/19006-capital-at.pdf
　　•used for Koalib
　　•F247 in nishiki-teki font
　　•F005 in Quivira

#	Musical Symbols Private-4

　MUSICAL SYMBOL ENLARGED DOUBLE FLAT

　　•indicates a major beat
　　•on the right of a tablature symbol in vertical layout, or above in horizontal layout

　CHINESE LUTE COMBINING DOT
　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•indicates that the string is to be plucked outwards
　　•on the right of a tablature symbol in vertical layout, or above in horizontal layout
◌	U+EC3D
　CHINESE LUTE COMBINING LEADING DOT
　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•indicates that the string is to be plucked with the index finger
　　•above a tablature symbol in vertical layout, or on the left in horizontal layout
◌	U+EC3E
　CHINESE LUTE COMBINING TRAILING DOT
　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•indicates that the string is to be plucked with the thumb
　　•beneath a tablature symbol in vertical layout, or on the right in horizontal layout
◌	U+EC3F
　CHINESE LUTE CHORD MARK
　　http://www.unicode.org/L2/L2017/17311-n4848-lute.pdf
　　•appended to the last character in a sequence of two to four tabalature symbols
representing a chord
　　•positioned on the right of a sequence of tabalature symbols in vertical layout, or above the sequence in horizontal layout

　　•looks like a small hollow star, but sits lower
	U+F561
　MINOR LIGHT
　　•sits lower than the black star
	U+F563
　PILE
　　= light
　　•similar dot is used on some charts for lights (with a light cone)
　　• When used in documents this and the preceding two characters are centered on a line slightly above the baseline, as are the position circles, glyphs in font may need adjustment
	U+F564
　LEADING LIGHTS
　　•two lights lining up at the bearing indicated in the charts
　　• character has no semantic connection to 2260 ≠ not equal to and is only superficially similar in appearance
　　→ 2260 ≠ not equal to
